                        var wasAlertBoxClosedYet =
                            window.Optanon != undefined && window.Optanon.IsAlertBoxClosed();
                        /**
                         * Code to automatically delete optional cookies after a user opts out.
                         * Code is adapted from https://my.onetrust.com/s/article/UUID-b2d72003-853b-e75b-e337-c6d26ea327eb?language=en_US
                         */
                        if (typeof OptanonWrapperCount == 'undefined') {
                            getInitialCookieGroups();
                        }
                        deleteCookieGroups(activeCookieGroups);

                        function getInitialCookieGroups() {
                            OptanonWrapperCount = "";
                            // OnetrustActiveGroups is defined by the OneTrust SDK.
                            activeCookieGroups = OnetrustActiveGroups;
                        }

                        function deleteCookieGroups(cookieGroups) {
                            var dataDomainGroups = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(Optanon.GetDomainData().Groups));
                            var deletedGroupIds = getInactiveGroupIds(cookieGroups, OnetrustActiveGroups);
                            if (deletedGroupIds.length != 0 && dataDomainGroups.length != 0) {
                                for (var i = 0; i < dataDomainGroups.length; i++) {
                                    var customGroupId = dataDomainGroups[i]['CustomGroupId'];
                                    if (customGroupId != '' &&
                                        deletedGroupIds.includes(customGroupId)
                                    ) {
                                        var domainGroupCookies = dataDomainGroups[i]['Cookies'];
                                        for (var j = 0; j < domainGroupCookies.length; j++) {
                                            var cookieName = domainGroupCookies[j].Name
                                            deleteCookieByNameForCurrentHost(cookieName);
                                        }
                                    }

                                    var domainGroupHosts = dataDomainGroups[i]['Hosts'];
                                    for (var j = 0; j < domainGroupHosts.length; j++) {
                                        var hostId = domainGroupHosts[j].HostId;
                                        var hostCookies = domainGroupHosts[j].Cookies;
                                        if (deletedGroupIds.includes(hostId)) {
                                            for (var k = 0; k < hostCookies.length; k++) {
                                                deleteCookieByNameForCurrentHost(hostCookies[k].Name);
                                            }
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                            getInitialCookieGroups(); // Reassign new group IDs
                        }

                        // Get inactive groups so we can delete them
                        function getInactiveGroupIds(customGroupId, activeGroup) {
                            // Initial OnetrustActiveGroups
                            customGroupId = customGroupId.split(',');
                            customGroupId = customGroupId.filter(Boolean);

                            // After action OnetrustActiveGroups
                            activeGroup = activeGroup.split(',');
                            activeGroup = activeGroup.filter(Boolean);

                            var result = [];
                            for (var i = 0; i < customGroupId.length; i++) {
                                if (activeGroup.indexOf(customGroupId[i]) <= -1) {
                                    result.push(customGroupId[i]);
                                }
                            }
                            return result;
                        }

                        function deleteCookieByNameForCurrentHost(cookieName) {
                            // Delete root path cookies
                            domainName = window.location.hostname;
                            var topLevelDomain = domainName;

                            if (domainName.startsWith('www.')) {
                                topLevelDomain = domainName.substr(4); // Remove "www."
                            } else if (domainName.startsWith('.')) {
                                topLevelDomain = domainName.substr(1); // Remove leading dot
                            }

                            // Modifying document.cookie like this will expire any cookies we set MaxAge for, since we're setting it to -99999999

                            var cookieMaxAgeToDeleteCookie = '-99999999';
                            var domainPrefixes = ['', '.', 'www.'];
                            for (var prefixIndex = 0; prefixIndex < domainPrefixes.length; prefixIndex++) {
                                var domainToExpireFor = domainPrefixes[prefixIndex] + topLevelDomain;
                                document.cookie = cookieName + '=; Max-Age=' + cookieMaxAgeToDeleteCookie + '; Path=/;Domain=' + topLevelDomain;
                                document.cookie = cookieName + '=; Max-Age=' + cookieMaxAgeToDeleteCookie + '; Path=/;';
                            }

                            // Delete the cookie from LocalStorage. We probably don't need this most of the time, but
                            // OneTrust recommends doing it anyway, in case vendors store data there
                            localStorage.removeItem(cookieName);

                            // Loop through path hierarchy and delete potential cookies at each path.
                            var pathArray = window.location.pathname.split('/');
                            for (var i = 0; i < pathArray.length; i++) {
                                if (pathArray[i]) {
                                    var currentPath = pathArray.slice(0, i + 1).join('/');
                                    document.cookie =
                                        cookieName + '=; Max-Age=' + cookieMaxAgeToDeleteCookie + '; Path=' + currentPath + ';Domain=' + topLevelDomain;
                                    document.cookie = cookieName+ '=; Max-Age=' + cookieMaxAgeToDeleteCookie + '; Path=' + currentPath + ';';
                                    // Account for trailing slash
                                    document.cookie =
                                        cookieName + '=; Max-Age=' + cookieMaxAgeToDeleteCookie + '; Path=' + currentPath + '/;Domain=' + topLevelDomain;
                                    document.cookie = cookieName + '=; Max-Age=' + cookieMaxAgeToDeleteCookie + '; Path=' + currentPath + '/;';
                                }
                            }
                        }

                        /**
                         * Code to automatically refresh the page when the user's consent status changes.
                         * Consent status is updated when the user clicks confirm/reject on the cookie banner.
                         * window.Optanon is the cookie banner SDK's global object.
                         */
                        if (window.Optanon != undefined) {
                            window.Optanon.OnConsentChanged(function (event) {
                                if (wasAlertBoxClosedYet == false) {
                                    window.location.reload();
                                }
                            });
                        }

rounded-huge-bottom"></div></div></div></div><div class="pt1"><div class="pb1">* Apps by Airtable are available for new qualified customers on our Business and Enterprise Scale plans who meet specific subscription.</div></div></div><div class="my4 col-12 max-width-3 mx-auto font-family-display-updated"><h2 class="center mb3 big huge strong">Have additional questions?</h2><div class="flex flex-wrap items-center mx-auto"><div class="sm-col-4 xs-col-12 mb2 center"><div class="mb1 strong caps quieter">Billing / pricing</div><a href="https://support.airtable.com/docs/airtable-billing-overview" class="h4 huge link text-blue text-blue-dark1-hover focus-visible" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Billing FAQ</a></div><div class="sm-col-4 xs-col-12 mb2 center"><div class="mb1 strong caps quieter">Special plans for</div><span class="items-center"><a href="https://airtable.com/shr9DxhP6lU9slZE6" class="h4 huge link text-blue text-blue-dark1-hover" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Nonprofits</a> <span class="big h4">or</span> <a href="https://airtable.com/shrtaLSBL0Z0sLQnX" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="h4 huge link text-blue text-blue-dark1-hover">Education</a></span></div><div class="sm-col-4 xs-col-12 mb2 center"><div class="mb1 strong caps quieter">Enterprise plans</div><div tabindex="0" role="button" class="h4 huge link text-blue text-blue-dark1-hover pointer">Contact Sales</div></div></div></div><div class="col-12"><h2 class="huge strong center big mb3 font-family-display-updated">Frequently asked questions</h2><div class="max-width-3 col-xs-12 mx-auto"><div class="col-12 flex flex-column line-height-4"><div class="understroke thick mb2 flex flex-column" id="pricing"><div class="flex pointer transparent focus-visible items-center mb1" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="answer-pricing"><p class="flex-auto heading-size-small stronger font-family-display-updated">How does Airtable's pricing work?</p><div class="flex" style="transition: transform 200ms;"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="flex-none icon" style="shape-rendering: geometricprecision;"><use fill="currentColor" href="/icons/icon_definitions.svg?v=68b23d569e0a0c2f5529fd9b824929e7#ChevronDown"></use></svg></div></div><div id="answer-pricing" class="hide"><div><div class="huge font-family-display-updated mt2 mb3">Airtable plans are charged per seat. If you are on Airtables Free plan, all users are free. If you are on a Team or Business plan, you will be charged for all users who have edit permissions for at least one base in the workspace. No charges will apply on a Team or Business plan for read-only collaborators, form submissions, or share links. Charges are prorated: users with edit permissions added partway through the month will only be charged for the days after they were added.</div></div></div></div><div class="understroke thick mb2 flex flex-column" id="enterprise"><div class="flex pointer transparent focus-visible items-center mb1" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="answer-enterprise"><p class="flex-auto heading-size-small stronger font-family-display-updated">How does Airtable's Business and Enterprise Scale pricing work?</p><div class="flex" style="transition: transform 200ms;"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="flex-none icon" style="shape-rendering: geometricprecision;"><use fill="currentColor" href="/icons/icon_definitions.svg?v=68b23d569e0a0c2f5529fd9b824929e7#ChevronDown"></use></svg></div></div><div id="answer-enterprise" class="hide"><div><div class="huge font-family-display-updated mt2 mb3">Airtable has two plans geared towards large company usage of Airtable: Business and Enterprise Scale. You can purchase Business either through the plan upgrades page in your workspace settings tab, or by contacting our sales team. To purchase Enterprise Scale, please contact sales. On either plan, you will be charged for all users with edit permissions for at least one base in your organization. As part of the Enterprise Scale plan, an organization has the ability to create unlimited org units, workspaces and bases within their organization. Charges are prorated: collaborators with edit permissions added partway through the billing cycle will only be charged for the months after they were added. For more information on our Business and Enterprise Scale plans, <div tabindex="0" role="button" class="pointer text-blue strong text-blue-dark1-hover focus-visible link inline">contact sales</div>.</div></div></div></div><div class="understroke thick mb2 flex flex-column" id="free"><div class="flex pointer transparent focus-visible items-center mb1" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="answer-free"><p class="flex-auto heading-size-small stronger font-family-display-updated">Is Airtable free to use?</p><div class="flex" style="transition: transform 200ms;"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="flex-none icon" style="shape-rendering: geometricprecision;"><use fill="currentColor" href="/icons/icon_definitions.svg?v=68b23d569e0a0c2f5529fd9b824929e7#ChevronDown"></use></svg></div></div><div id="answer-free" class="hide"><div><div class="huge font-family-display-updated mt2 mb3">Airtable has multiple packages to help teams of all sizes orchestrate their work. Our Free plan is available to teams for no charge and provides the key building blocks to help you build applications. The Free plan is formulated for individual users, very small teams, or those with lightweight needs. Our paid plans offer additional power and scale for teams, departments, and large enterprises.</div></div></div></div><div class="understroke thick mb2 flex flex-column" id="cost"><div class="flex pointer transparent focus-visible items-center mb1" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="answer-cost"><p class="flex-auto heading-size-small stronger font-family-display-updated">How much does Airtable cost?</p><div class="flex" style="transition: transform 200ms;"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="flex-none icon" style="shape-rendering: geometricprecision;"><use fill="currentColor" href="/icons/icon_definitions.svg?v=68b23d569e0a0c2f5529fd9b824929e7#ChevronDown"></use></svg></div></div><div id="answer-cost" class="hide"><div><div class="huge font-family-display-updated mt2 mb3">Our Free plan is available at no cost for users just getting started. For teams who like the features of our Free plan but need more capacity, our Team plan is available for $20/user/month when billed annually. Our Business and Enterprise Scale plans include the additional customization, data scale, flexibility, and administrative features that departments and enterprise organizations need. Business is available at $45/user/month when billed annually our Enterprise Scale plan pricing is custom, based on the organizations needs and scale with Airtable. To learn more about our Enterprise Scale pricing, <div tabindex="0" role="button" class="pointer text-blue strong text-blue-dark1-hover focus-visible link inline">contact sales</div>.</div></div></div></div><div class="understroke thick mb2 flex flex-column" id="paymentOptions"><div class="flex pointer transparent focus-visible items-center mb1" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="answer-paymentOptions"><p class="flex-auto heading-size-small stronger font-family-display-updated">What are my payment options?</p><div class="flex" style="transition: transform 200ms;"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="flex-none icon" style="shape-rendering: geometricprecision;"><use fill="currentColor" href="/icons/icon_definitions.svg?v=68b23d569e0a0c2f5529fd9b824929e7#ChevronDown"></use></svg></div></div><div id="answer-paymentOptions" class="hide"><div><div class="huge font-family-display-updated mt2 mb3">All payments are made via credit card for Team workspaces, and for Business if purchased through your workspace settings tab. For Business and Enterprise Scale accounts purchased through our sales team, we can issue an annual invoice with payment via PO and/or ACH, wire, or check. Please <div tabindex="0" role="button" class="pointer text-blue strong text-blue-dark1-hover focus-visible link inline">contact sales</div> for more information.</div></div></div></div><div class="understroke thick mb2 flex flex-column" id="limits"><div class="flex pointer transparent focus-visible items-center mb1" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="answer-limits"><p class="flex-auto heading-size-small stronger font-family-display-updated">What happens when I hit my usage limits?</p><div class="flex" style="transition: transform 200ms;"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="flex-none icon" style="shape-rendering: geometricprecision;"><use fill="currentColor" href="/icons/icon_definitions.svg?v=68b23d569e0a0c2f5529fd9b824929e7#ChevronDown"></use></svg></div></div><div id="answer-limits" class="hide"><div><div class="huge font-family-display-updated mt2 mb3">If you reach (or are over) our record or attachment limits, youll still be able to use your bases and we will never remove your data. Well notify you of the overage and you will not be able to add more records or attachments until you upgrade to a new plan. For automations and API limits, you will be capped at the usage limit on your current plan. </div></div></div></div><div class="understroke thick mb2 flex flex-column" id="legacyEnterprise"><div class="flex pointer transparent focus-visible items-center mb1" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="answer-legacyEnterprise"><p class="flex-auto heading-size-small stronger font-family-display-updated">I am currently on Airtables legacy Enterprise plan  where can I see a list of my current features?</p><div class="flex" style="transition: transform 200ms;"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="flex-none icon" style="shape-rendering: geometricprecision;"><use fill="currentColor" href="/icons/icon_definitions.svg?v=68b23d569e0a0c2f5529fd9b824929e7#ChevronDown"></use></svg></div></div><div id="answer-legacyEnterprise" class="hide"><div><div class="huge font-family-display-updated mt2 mb3">For existing customers on Airtables legacy Enterprise plan, no changes will go into effect until your renewal, at which point your account team will discuss your plan options with you. In the meantime, see this <a href="https://support.airtable.com/docs/enterprise-legacy-plan-information" class="pointer text-blue strong text-blue-dark1-hover focus-visible" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">help article</a> for a list of your current features and functionality.</div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="h-s-footer-props"         const driftWidgetFrame = driftWidget.querySelector('iframe');
        const widgetStyle = driftWidget.style;
        const frameOrigin = "https:\u002F\u002Fstatic.airtable.com";

        /** Snippet for the parent page to properly resize the iframe and pass context */

        driftWidgetFrame.onload = function() {
            const widgetFrameWindow = driftWidgetFrame.contentWindow;
            const widgetStyle = driftWidget.style;
            widgetFrameWindow.postMessage({
                kind: 'init',
                data: {driftSettings: {"appId":"kuidevm857pc","shouldEnableDrift":true}},
            }, frameOrigin);

            function getShareablePageContext() {
                const ALLOWED_URL_SHARING_PATHNAME_PREFIXES = ["\u002Fsolutions","\u002Fproduct","\u002Fintegrations","\u002Fenterprise","\u002Fpricing","\u002Fcontact-sales"];
                const isPagenamePrefixInAllowedList = window.location.pathname === '/' || ALLOWED_URL_SHARING_PATHNAME_PREFIXES.some(
                    function(allowedPrefix) {
                        const pathname = window.location.pathname;
                        // startsWith is not supported by IE, doing this check manually
                        return  pathname === allowedPrefix || pathname.indexOf(allowedPrefix + '/') === 0;
                    }
                );
                const windowLocation =  {
                    hash: window.location.hash,
                    host: window.location.host,
                    hostname: window.location.hostname,
                    href: window.location.href,
                    origin: window.location.origin,
                    pathname: window.location.pathname,
                    port: window.location.port,
                    protocol: window.location.protocol,
                    search: window.location.search
                };
                return {
                    window: {
                        location: isPagenamePrefixInAllowedList ? windowLocation : {},
                        navigator: {
                            language: window.navigator.language,
                            browserLanguage: window.navigator.browserLanguage,
                            userAgent: window.navigator.userAgent
                        },
                        innerHeight: Math.min(630, window.innerHeight),
                        innerWidth: Math.min(365, window.innerWidth)
                    },
                    document: {
                        title: isPagenamePrefixInAllowedList ? document.title : 'Private Page',
                    },
                }
            }

            window.addEventListener('message', function (event) {
                // Only process events from the appropriate domain and iframe.
                if (
                    event.source !== widgetFrameWindow ||
                    event.origin !== "https:\u002F\u002Fstatic.airtable.com"
                ) {
                    return;
                }
                if  (!(driftWidgetFrame && driftWidgetFrame.contentWindow) && event.source === driftWidgetFrame.contentWindow) {
                    return
                }

                // on startup - pass created context into iframe

                // If the drift chat widget is off, then drift may still be used for tracking
                // In this case, we will disable in-product chat functionality
                const shouldEnableDriftChatWidget = true;
                if (event.data && typeof event.data === 'object') {
                    const data = event.data.data;
                    const kind = event.data.kind;
                    switch(kind) {
                        case 'driftShow':
                            if(!shouldEnableDriftChatWidget) {
                                break;
                            }
                            widgetStyle.opacity = '1';
                            widgetStyle.pointerEvents = 'auto';
                            window.driftTracker && window.driftTracker.trackShow && window.driftTracker.trackShow();
                            break;
                        case 'driftChatOpen':
                            widgetStyle.opacity = '1';
                            widgetStyle.pointerEvents = 'auto';
                            widgetStyle.height = '630px';
                            widgetStyle.width = '365px';
                            window.driftTracker && window.driftTracker.trackOpen && window.driftTracker.trackOpen();
                            break;
                        case 'driftMinimize':
                            widgetStyle.height = '120px';
                            widgetStyle.width = '354px';
                            window.driftTracker && window.driftTracker.trackMinimize && window.driftTracker.trackMinimize();
                            break;
                        case 'driftHide':
                            widgetStyle.opacity = '0';
                            widgetStyle.pointerEvents = 'none';
                            window.driftTracker && window.driftTracker.trackClose && window.driftTracker.trackClose();
                            break;
                        case 'driftIframeReady':
                            var context = getShareablePageContext();
                            driftWidgetFrame.contentWindow.postMessage({ kind: 'driftSetContext', data: context }, frameOrigin);
                            break;
                        case 'driftPlaybookFired':
                            window.driftTracker && window.driftTracker.trackPlaybookFired && window.driftTracker.trackPlaybookFired();
                            break;
                        case 'driftStartConversation':
                            window.driftTracker && window.driftTracker.trackStartConversation && window.driftTracker.trackStartConversation();
                            break;
                        case 'driftMessageReceived':
                            window.driftTracker && window.driftTracker.trackMessageReceived && window.driftTracker.trackMessageReceived();
                            break;
                        case 'driftMessageSent':
                            window.driftTracker && window.driftTracker.trackMessageSent && window.driftTracker.trackMessageSent();
                            break;
                        default:
                            console.error("Unrecognized event kind '" + kind + "'");
                            break;
                    }
                }
            });
            widgetStyle.display = 'block';
        };
    })();
    </script></div><script nonce="">

                    cookieSettingsButton.style.display = 'inline-block';

                }
